# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
you write in x, find the derivative, rewrite as the reciprocal, simplify ^r293YXei

it is a square matrix made of a diagonal of 1 ^KrEBLYss

it acts like the number 1, if you multiply by it another
matrix you get the other matrix back ^VZ8YwWCU

a sequence where each member is expressed as a function of n ^NXwPbwdu

a sequence where each number is added by a constant ^rRpFxmxH

a sequence where each number is multiplied by a constant ^rlVcAcmp

it is the constant by which each member is multiplied in a geometric sequence ^WGHRAyKA

arithmetic sequence ^fpzJ8g01

a line ^Phx6jPSt

geometric sequence ^PMSqruhm

an exponential curve ^tB6EAYnn

initial term ^MKj8kEmV

common ratio ^vsQcJEVI
